//　あるいは魅音なりのドツキ漫才なのだろうか＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　あるいは魅音なりのドツキ漫才なのだろうか。",
		   NULL, "Ou então isso vai acabar sendo A Hora da Comédia do Espancamento de Mion.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//　だとしたらえらい命懸けだぞ...￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　だとしたらえらい命懸けだぞ…。",
		   NULL, "Se isso acontecer, o resultado seria fatal...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//「挫けるなよ魅音。レナのジャブを見切れるのはお前しかいない！＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#956f6e>圭一</color>", NULL, "<color=#956f6e>Keiichi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 1, "ps3/s19/01/hr_kei01260", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「挫けるなよ魅音。レナのジャブを見切れるのはお前しかいない！」",
		   NULL, "\"Não sinta-se mal, Mion. Você é provavelmente a única que pode se desviar de seus jabs!\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//「......私は膝じゃないかと思ってんだけどね......。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>魅音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Mion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 3, "ps3/s19/03/990300075", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……私は膝じゃないかと思ってんだけどね……。」",
		   NULL, "\"...Parecia até que era o joelho dela...\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　...俺たちはとんでもない格闘王とお付き合いしてるんじゃないだろうか＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…俺たちはとんでもない格闘王とお付き合いしてるんじゃないだろうか？",
		   NULL, "...Será que estávamos andando com um mestre das artes marciais sem rival?", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//　将来、エクストリームな世界でデビューするかもしれないな...￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　将来、エクストリームな世界でデビューするかもしれないな…。",
		   NULL, "Talvez algum dia vejamos seu debut num esporte de extremo contato...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//「レナには負けられないぞ！　魅音も鍛えてリベンジだ！＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#956f6e>圭一</color>", NULL, "<color=#956f6e>Keiichi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 1, "ps3/s19/01/hr_kei01270", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「レナには負けられないぞ！　魅音も鍛えてリベンジだ！」",
		   NULL, "\"Você não pode perder para Rena! Você tem de treinar e ter uma revanche!\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//「け!w300......圭ちゃんがしてよ!s300......!sd。おじさんは応援してる......。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>魅音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Mion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 3, "ps3/s19/03/990300076", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「け",
		   NULL, "\"Kei...", Line_Continue);

	// (backup) SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 300 );
	// (backup) SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "……圭ちゃんがしてよ……。",
		   NULL, " Kei-chan, você deveria...", Line_Continue);

	SetSpeedOfMessage( TRUE, 0 );

	OutputLine(NULL, "おじさんは応援してる……。」",
		   NULL, " Oji-san vai torcer por você...\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));

	SetSpeedOfMessage( FALSE, 0 );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　俺と魅音はレナの必殺技攻略への決意を新たにするのだった...￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　俺と魅音はレナの必殺技攻略への決意を新たにするのだった…。",
		   NULL, "Mion e eu reafirmamos nossa determinação em descobrir um jeito de contra-atacar a técnica infalível de Rena...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//☆ここで幕間かな。
//　ここまでの過程での選択肢等でまたチップスが手に入っているのだろう。
//　チップスとしては...「誰か（誰がいいかな？）の日記」とか「保護者の方へ」とかなんとかその辺り。

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
//	DrawBustshot( 5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
//	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene("black", 3000 );

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/onik001", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
